   <section class="pl-anchor-tabs--section pl-spacer pl-spacer--cut-left pl-spacer--cut-right pl-spacer--in--small pl-spacer--out--small pl-bg pl-bg--gray-lightest">
    <div class="container">
     <div class="row pl-push pl-push--mobile--smallest pl-push--tablet--smallest pl-push--desktop--smallest">
      <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-10 col-md-offset-1 col-lg-8 col-lg-offset-2 pl-lockup text-center">
       <h2 class="pl-h2 pl-spacer--in--smallest pl-spacer--cut-top pl-spacer--cut-h">
        Service &amp; Support offered by Third Party Companies
       </h2>
       <p class="pl-text pl-text--medium">
       </p>
       <p class="pl-text pl-text--medium" style="text-align: left;">
        At times, third-parties offering support on Canon products can look authentic but please be vigilant - these websites are not associated with Canon and Canon does not endorse their services.
       </p>
       <br/>
       <p class="pl-text pl-text--medium" style="text-align: left;">
        Examples include:
        <strong>
         https://canon.com-ijsetup.com/ij-start-cannon/; https://www.ijcanon.co.uk/; https://ij-start-canon.us/ and https://ijstartcanons.com/
        </strong>
        .
       </p>
       <br/>
       <p class="pl-text pl-text--medium" style="text-align: left;">
        If you want to get free support from Canon, please contact us through our Canon support contact centre.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="pl-btn pl-btn--blue pl-btn--medium" data-tealiumevent="Generic Link (default)" data-tealiumeventmetadata="Contact Support" href="/support/consumer_products/contact_support/" target="_self">
         Contact Support
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>
     </div>
